###########################################
#
# Plot Events
#
# ID 7000-8299 is reserved
#
###########################################
# Blackmail									7250-7270
# Drunken Plot Member						7040-7045
#
# Ultimatum event series					8000-8120
# Plot to kill character 					8150-8227
#
# Assassination notification events			8250-8299
#											7700-7999

# Events disabled/unused in CK2Plus:
# 8000, 8005, 8010, 8015, 8020, 8025, 8026, 8027, 8028,
# 8029, 8030, 8031, 8035, 8050, 8055, 8060, 8065, 8066,
# 8067, 8068, 8069, 8070, 8071, 8075, 8076, 8080, 8081,
# 8085, 8086, 8090, 8091, 8095, 8094, 8096, 8097, 8093,
# 8114, 8115, 8116, 8117, 8118, 8119


###########################################
# Blackmail
###########################################
# 7250-7270

# The plot has been leaked
character_event = {
	id = 7250
	desc = EVTDESC7250
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		has_plot = yes
		num_of_plot_backers >= 1
		is_plot_active = no

		job_spymaster = {
			NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
		}

		top_liege = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				is_playable = yes

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value < 0
				}

				NOR = {
					character = ROOT
					is_liege_of = ROOT
					is_plot_target_of = ROOT

					employer = {
						character = ROOT
					}

					any_backed_character = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 20

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.85

			any_plot_backer = {
				trait = imbecile
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.85

			any_plot_backer = {
				trait = lunatic
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			num_of_plot_backers >= 2
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			num_of_plot_backers >= 4
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			num_of_plot_backers >= 6
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			num_of_plot_backers >= 8
		}

		# CK2Plus
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 10
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 15
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 20
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7250

		hidden_effect = {
			random_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes

					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value < 0
					}

					NOR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						is_plot_target_of = ROOT

						any_backed_character = {
							character = ROOT
						}

						employer = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}

				letter_event = {
					id = 7255
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail or not
letter_event = {
	id = 7255
	desc = EVTDESC7255
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			reveal_plot = ROOT
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7255 # A little blackmail can't hurt

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = {
				id = 7260
				days = 1
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7260
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50

			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					plot_target_char = {
						NOR = {
							is_rival = ROOT
							has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
							is_allied_with = ROOT
							is_friend = ROOT
						}

						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value >= -25
						}

						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value < 50
						}
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2

				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value < -25
				}
			}

			# CK2Plus
			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = envious
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7255 # It does not concern me

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = slothful
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = content
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1

				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC7255 # Reveal it

		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					plot_target_char = {
						job_spymaster = { always = yes }
					}
				}

				reveal_plot_w_message = yes
			}
			else = {
				reveal_plot = yes
			}

			plot_target_char = {
				show_scope_change = no

				opinion = {
					name = devious_plotter
					who = PREV
					years = 10
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						independent = no
						NOT = { vassal_of = PREV }
					}

					liege = {
						show_scope_change = no

						opinion = {
							name = devious_plotter
							who = PREVPREV
							years = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30

			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					plot_target_char = {
						NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }

						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value < -25
						}
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = just
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = diligent
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2

				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value < -25
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bounce event (when blackmail done by diplo-action)
character_event = {
	id = 7259

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 7260 }
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail attempt
letter_event = {
	id = 7260
	desc = EVTDESC7260

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7260 # Give in

		wealth = -100

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_blackmailed
			who = FROM
			years = 10
		}

		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = 7265
				days = 3
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				wealth < 100
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				wealth >= 250
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = paranoid
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = deceitful
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7260 # I won't tolerate blackmail!

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_failed_blackmail
			who = FROM
			multiplier = 2
			years = 10
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					job_spymaster = { always = yes }
				}
			}

			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		else = {
			reveal_plot = yes
		}

		plot_target_char = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = devious_plotter
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					independent = no
					NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT }
				}

				liege = {
					show_scope_change = no

					opinion = {
						name = devious_plotter
						who = ROOT
						years = 10
					}
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = 7270
				days = 1
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = craven
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail succeeded
letter_event = {
	id = 7265
	desc = EVTDESC7265

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT

		wealth = 100
		clr_character_flag = attempted_blackmail
	}
}

# Blackmail failed
letter_event = {
	id = 7270
	desc = EVTDESC7270

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7270

		clr_character_flag = attempted_blackmail
	}
}

###########################################
# Drunken Plot Member
###########################################
# 7040-7045

# Drunk plot member spills the beans - Non-Murder Plots
character_event = {
	id = 7040
	desc = EVTDESC7040
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = temperate }
		is_smart_trigger = no

		any_backed_character = {
			NOR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				has_character_flag = event7040

				plot_target_char = {
					any_known_plotter = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}

			is_plot_active = no

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { religion_group = muslim }

				OR = {
					trait = hedonist
					trait = drunkard
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 25

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = drunkard
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = imbecile
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			OR = {
				trait = slow
				trait = dull
			}
		}

		# mult_modifier = {
		# 	factor = 10.0
		# 	trait = temperate
		# }
		#
		# mult_modifier = {
		# 	factor = 2.0
		# 	trait = genius
		# }
		#
		# mult_modifier = {
		# 	factor = 1.5
		#
		# 	OR = {
		# 		trait = quick
		# 		trait = shrewd
		# 	}
		# }

		# CK2Plus
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = honest
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = deceitful
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = paranoid
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = craven
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = trusting
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			intrigue < 5
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 8
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 10
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 15
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 20
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7040

		random_backed_character = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
					has_character_flag = event7040

					plot_target_char = {
						any_known_plotter = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
			}

			opinion = {
				name = revealed_plot
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}

			set_character_flag = event7040

			character_event = {
				id = 7045
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Plot revealed by drunken backer
character_event = {
	id = 7045
	desc = EVTDESC7045
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7045

		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					job_spymaster = { always = yes }
				}
			}

			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		else = {
			reveal_plot = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_plot = plot_seduce }
			}

			plot_target_char = {
				show_scope_change = no

				opinion = {
					name = devious_plotter
					who = ROOT
					years = 10
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						independent = no
						NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT }
					}

					liege = {
						show_scope_change = no

						opinion = {
							name = devious_plotter
							who = ROOT
							years = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Drunk plot member spills the beans - Murder Plots
character_event = {
	id = 7041
	desc = EVTDESC7040
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = temperate }
		is_smart_trigger = no

		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}

			is_plot_active = no

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { religion_group = muslim }

				OR = {
					trait = hedonist
					trait = drunkard
				}
			}

			NOR = {
				has_character_flag = event7041

				plot_target_char = {
					any_known_plotter = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = drunkard
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = imbecile
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			OR = {
				trait = slow
				trait = dull
			}
		}

		# mult_modifier = {
		# 	factor = 10.0
		# 	trait = temperate
		# }
		#
		# mult_modifier = {
		# 	factor = 2.0
		# 	trait = genius
		# }
		#
		# mult_modifier = {
		# 	factor = 1.5
		#
		# 	OR = {
		# 		trait = quick
		# 		trait = shrewd
		# 	}
		# }

		# CK2Plus
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = honest
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = deceitful
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = paranoid
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = craven
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = trusting
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			intrigue < 5
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 8
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 10
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 15
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue >= 20
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7040

		random_backed_character = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}

				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = event7041

					plot_target_char = {
						any_known_plotter = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
			}

			opinion = {
				name = revealed_plot
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}

			set_character_flag = event7041

			character_event = {
				id = 7046
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Murder plot revealed by drunken backer
character_event = {
	id = 7046
	desc = EVTDESC7045
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7045

		clr_character_flag = event7041

		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					job_spymaster = { always  = yes }
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		else = {
			reveal_plot = yes
		}

		plot_target_char = {
			show_scope_change = no

			save_event_target_as = target_victim

			ROOT = {
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}

			clear_event_target = target_victim

			opinion = {
				name = devious_plotter
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					independent = no
					NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT }
				}

				liege = {
					show_scope_change = no

					opinion = {
						name = devious_plotter
						who = ROOT
						years = 10
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				independent = no

				NOR = {
					trait = lunatic
					trait = possessed
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}
			}

			cancel_plot = yes
		}
	}
}

###########################################
# Ultimatum event series
###########################################
# 8000-8120

### Ultimatum events

# Ultimatum - gain a title
letter_event = {
	id = 8000
	desc = EVTDESC8000

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = { id = 8050 }

			any_plot_backer = {
				letter_event = { id = 8070 }
			}

			plot_target_title = {
				show_scope_change = no
				usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = PREV
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			trigger = {
				FROM = { plot_power >= 1.0 }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8000

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = {
				id = 8100
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8100
			}

			tooltip = {
				any_plot_backer = {
					count = 10
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				FROM = { plot_power >= 1.5 }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { plot_power >= 2.0 }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { plot_power >= 3.0 }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { plot_power >= 4.0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - seniority
letter_event = {
	id = 8005
	desc = EVTDESC8005

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			in_faction = faction_succ_seniority
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes

			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_succ_seniority

				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

		}

			}
		}

					faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective

					letter_event = { id = 8085 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			faction_succ_feudal_elective = { # The target (title) of the faction
				set_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss

				if = {
					limit = {

							title = e_hre

							faction = faction_independence
							power >= 0.75
						}

						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_independence
							power < 1.5
						}
					}

					random_list = {
						75 = { }

						5 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45000 # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}

						20 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45004 # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.75

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_independence
						power >= 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_independence
						power >= 1.5
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_independence
						power >= 2.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_independence
						power >= 3.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_independence
						power >= 4.0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - Install Pretender
letter_event = {
	id = 8036
	desc = EVTDESC8036

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			leads_faction = faction_pretender
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_leader
			clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_member
			clr_character_flag = will_join_civil_war

			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_pretender

				diplomatic_immunity = yes
				clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_member
				clr_character_flag = will_join_civil_war
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000 # Give in

		log = "[Root.GetBestName] has caved to the claimant faction demand of [From.GetBestName]."

		hidden_effect = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					vassal_of = ROOT

					NOR = {
						in_faction = faction_pretender
						character = FROM
						character = ROOT
					}
				}

				character_event = { id = 8099 }
			}

			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8061 }
				diplomatic_immunity = no

				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_pretender

					letter_event = { id = 8098 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5

			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power >= 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.001
				has_nickname = nick_the_conqueror
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}

			# CK2Plus
			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 5

				FROM = {
					supported_claimant_title = {
						is_primary_holder_title = no
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					supported_claimant_title = {
						is_primary_holder_title = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8000

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_pretender
							power >= 1.0
						}
					}
				}

				random = {
					chance = 25

					character_event = {
						id = 45002 # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
						months = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		log = "[Root.GetBestName] has refused the claimant faction demand of [From.GetBestName] -- this should start a civil war."

		set_character_flag = faction_pretender_war

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_pretender
					count = 10
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				letter_event = { id = 8111 } # Inform

				# Setup faction leader
				diplomatic_immunity = no
				clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
				set_character_flag = original_war_liege
				pf_setup_rebel_effect = yes

				# Setup faction backers
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_pretender

					diplomatic_immunity = no
					pf_setup_rebel_effect = yes

					supported_claimant = {
						opinion = {
							name = opinion_very_grateful
							who = PREV
							years = 10
						}

						reverse_opinion = {
							name = opinion_fought_for_claimant
							who = PREV
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}

				supported_claimant = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { character = PREV }
						}
					}

					opinion = {
						name = opinion_very_grateful
						who = PREV
						years = 10
					}

					reverse_opinion = {
						name = opinion_fought_for_claimant
						who = PREV
						years = 20
					}

					# Call claimant into war, if possible
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT }
						}

						character_event = {
							id = PlusFaction.423
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}

			# Start the actual war
			if = {
				limit = { character = supported_claimant }

				faction_pretender = { # The target (title) of the faction
					reverse_war = {
						target = FROM
						casus_belli = claim_on_liege_plot
						faction = faction_pretender
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				faction_pretender = { # The target (title) of the faction
					reverse_war = {
						target = FROM
						casus_belli = other_claim_on_liege_plot
						faction = faction_pretender
					}
				}
			}
		}

		# Inform remaining vassals
		any_vassal = {
			letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.403 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.75

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power >= 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power >= 1.5
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power >= 2.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power >= 3.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power >= 4.0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Demand accepted - Install Claimant
letter_event = {
	id = 8061
	desc = EVTDESC8061

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
		clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_leader
		clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_member
		clr_character_flag = will_join_civil_war

		supported_claimant = {
			save_event_target_as = claimant

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_very_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_fought_for_claimant
				who = ROOT
				years = 20
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT

		supported_claimant = {
			show_scope_change = no

			if = {
				limit = {
					prisoner = yes

					host = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_vassal_or_below_of = FROM
						}
					}
				}

				imprison = no
			}
		}

		supported_claimant_title = {
			show_scope_change = no

			# If the claimant has the wrong government type, take care of that first.
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:claimant = {
						is_ruler = yes
						lower_real_tier_than = PREV

						OR = {
							is_theocracy = yes
							is_republic = yes
						}
					}

					holder_scope = {
						OR = {
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
							is_nomadic = yes
						}
					}
				}

				event_target:claimant = {
					show_scope_change = no

					abdicate = { move = no }
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { is_primary_holder_title = yes }

				FROM = {
					show_scope_change = no

					any_demesne_title = {
						show_scope_change = no

						limit =	{ is_crown_law_title = yes }

						set_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss

						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_law

							crown_authority_1 = { add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_0 }
							crown_authority_2 = { add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_1 }
							crown_authority_3 = { add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_2 }
							crown_authority_4 = { add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_3 }
						}

						clr_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss
					}

					any_demesne_title = {
						show_scope_change = no

						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_law = tribal_organization_1
								has_law = tribal_organization_2
								has_law = tribal_organization_3
								has_law = tribal_organization_4
							}
						}

						set_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss

						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_law

							tribal_organization_1 = { add_law_w_cooldown = tribal_organization_0 }
							tribal_organization_2 = { add_law_w_cooldown = tribal_organization_1 }
							tribal_organization_3 = { add_law_w_cooldown = tribal_organization_2 }
							tribal_organization_4 = { add_law_w_cooldown = tribal_organization_3 }
						}

						clr_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss
					}

					any_demesne_title = {
						show_scope_change = no

						limit = {
							is_primary_holder_title_tier = yes
							is_primary_holder_title = no
						}

						usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = {
							target = event_target:claimant
							type = faction_demand
						}
					}

					primary_title = {
						show_scope_change = no

						usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = {
							target = event_target:claimant
							type = faction_demand
						}

						hidden_effect = {
							make_primary_title = yes
						}
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						# Usurp capital if possible
						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									higher_real_tier_than >= COUNT
									num_of_count_titles >= 2
								}

								event_target:claimant = {
									primary_title = {
										NOT = { has_law = succ_feudal_elective }

										FROM = {
											capital_scope = {
												de_jure_liege_or_above = PREVPREV
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}

							capital_scope = {
								county = {
									usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = {
										target = event_target:claimant
										type = faction_demand
									}
								}
							}
						}

						set_defacto_liege = event_target:claimant
						pf_liege_change_effect = yes

						# Transfer FROM's non-dejure vassals to claimant
						any_vassal = {
							limit = {
								primary_title = {
									NOT = {	de_jure_liege_or_above = PREVPREV } # FROM
								}
							}

							set_defacto_liege = event_target:claimant
							pf_liege_change_effect = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss

				if = {
					limit = { is_crown_law_title = yes }

					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_law

						crown_authority_1 = { add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_0 }
						crown_authority_2 = { add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_1 }
						crown_authority_3 = { add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_2 }
						crown_authority_4 = { add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_3 }
					}
				}

				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_law

					tribal_organization_1 = { add_law_w_cooldown = tribal_organization_0 }
					tribal_organization_2 = { add_law_w_cooldown = tribal_organization_1 }
					tribal_organization_3 = { add_law_w_cooldown = tribal_organization_2 }
					tribal_organization_4 = { add_law_w_cooldown = tribal_organization_3 }
				}

				clr_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss

				usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded_and_vassals_no_adj = {
					target = event_target:claimant
					type = faction_demand
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisoned Wine
character_event = {
	id = 8150
	desc = EVTDESC8150
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	portrait = event_target:plot_target

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}

		is_plot_active = no

		plot_target_char = {
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			block_general_event_trigger = no
			is_murder_quest_target_of_root_trigger = no

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { religion_group = muslim }

				OR = {
					trait = decadent
					trait = hedonist
					trait = drunkard
				}
			}
		}

		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power >= 0.025
		}
	}

		months = 500

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT

			}

# Poisoned Wine - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8155
	desc = EVTDESC8155
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8155 # Drinks the wine

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = temperate }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = gluttonous }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 8156 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 8163 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 8163 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 8157 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 8164 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 8164 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8155 # Discovers the poison

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = temperate }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = gluttonous }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 8158 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 8165 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 8165 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 8159 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 8166 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 8166 days = 1 } }

				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}
			}

			activate_plot = no
		}
	}
}

					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}

				plot_target_char = {
					check_variable = {
						which = personal_spy_network
						value >= 30
					}

					has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network
					is_adult = no
					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}

				plot_target_char = {
					check_variable = {
						which = personal_spy_network
						value >= 40
					}

					has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network
					is_adult = no
					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}

				plot_target_char = {
					check_variable = {
						which = personal_spy_network
						value >= 50
					}

					has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network
					is_adult = no
					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = plot_backer

		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}

				is_plot_active = no
				plot_power >= 0.5

				plot_target_char = {
					is_adult = no
					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}

				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV
						power >= 0.025
					}
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = plot_leader

			plot_target_char = {
				save_event_target_as = plot_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8170 # The conspirators provide a killer

		trigger = {
			event_target:plot_leader = {
				plot_power >= 1.0
			}
		}

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			show_scope_change = no

			activate_plot = yes

			character_event = {
				id = 8180
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8160
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8171 # Ask the Plotter for funds

		trigger = {
			intrigue < 10

			event_target:plot_leader = {
				plot_power < 1.0
			}
		}

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			show_scope_change = no

			activate_plot = yes

			character_event = {
				id = 8172
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8152
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8170 # Bribe a Guard

		trigger = {
			intrigue < 10

			event_target:plot_leader = {
				plot_power < 1.0
			}
		}

		scaled_wealth = -0.5

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			show_scope_change = no

			activate_plot = yes

			character_event = {
				id = 8180
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8160
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

# Falling Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8175
	desc = EVTDESC8175
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8175 # Falls

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 8176 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 8183 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 8183 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 8177 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 8184 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 8184 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8175 # Dodges

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 8178 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 8185 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 8185 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 8179 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 8186 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 8186 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Liege is approached by Plotter
letter_event = {
	id = 7500
	desc = EVTDESC7500

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
			vassal_of = ROOT
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = plot_liege

		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = plot_leader

			plot_target_char = {
				save_event_target_as = plot_target
			}

			plot_target_title = {
				save_event_target_as = plot_title
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7500 # Yes

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = {
				id = 7501
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7501
			}

			event_target:plot_target = {
				show_scope_change = no

				letter_event = {
					id = 7504
					days = 4
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7504A
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			trigger = {
				NOT = { trait = just }

				opinion = {
					who = event_target:plot_leader
					value >= -10
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				trait = deceitful
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				likes_better_than = {
					who = event_target:plot_target
					than = event_target:plot_leader
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7500 # No

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = {
				id = 7502
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7502
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				likes_better_than = {
					who = event_target:plot_leader
					than = event_target:plot_target
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = EVTDESC7504

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
			vassal_of = event_target:plot_liege
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7504 # Take it!

		trigger = {
			any_vassal = {
				real_tier = COUNT

				any_demesne_title = {
					real_tier = COUNT
					de_jure_liege = event_target:plot_title
				}
			}
		}

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			set_character_flag = weaken_vassal
			plot_succeeds = yes
		}

		random_vassal = {

			limit = {
				real_tier = COUNT

				any_demesne_title = {
					real_tier = COUNT
					de_jure_liege = event_target:plot_title
				}
			}

			usurp_title = event_target:plot_title
		}

		liege = {
			letter_event = { id = 7508 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7504 # Never

		liege = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = {
				id = 7509
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7509
			}
		}
	}

			opinion = {

				years = 5
			}

		}
	}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Archer Ambush
character_event = {
	id = 7700
	desc = EVTDESC7700

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {

			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 7705
				days = 30
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7705

		}
	}

		trigger = {

			save_event_target_as = plot_leader

			plot_target_char = {
				save_event_target_as = plot_target
			}
		}

# Archer Ambush - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7705
	desc = EVTDESC7705
	picture = GFX_evt_longbowman
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7705 # Hit by arrows

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = craven }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7706 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7713 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7713 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7707 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7714 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7714 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7705 # Avoids arrows

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = craven }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7708 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7715 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7715 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7709 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7716 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7716 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Manure Explosion
character_event = {
	id = 7720
	desc = EVTDESC7720
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	portrait = event_target:plot_target

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}

		is_plot_active = no

		plot_target_char = {
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			block_general_event_trigger = no
			is_murder_quest_target_of_root_trigger = no
		}

		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power >= 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.10
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

				plotter = ROOT

# Manure Explosion - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7725
	desc = EVTDESC7725
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7725 # Blown up

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7726 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7733 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7733 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7727 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7734 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7734 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7725 # Not blown up

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7728 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7735 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7735 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7729 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7736 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7736 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

character_event = {

	desc = EVTDESC7740

	only_capable = yes

			practical_age < 5

		}

			character_event = {
				id = 7752

			}

			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 7745
				days = 30

			}
		}
	}

# Infanticide - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7745
	desc = EVTDESC7745
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7745 # Smothered

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = brave }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = gregarious }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7746 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7753 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7753 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7747 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7754 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7754 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7745 # Not smothered

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = brave }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = gregarious }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7748 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7755 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7755 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7749 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7756 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7756 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### PRISON BREAK - PRISONERS ONLY
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Prison Break
character_event = {
	id = 7760
	desc = EVTDESC7760
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	portrait = event_target:plot_target

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}

		is_plot_active = no

		plot_target_char = {
			prisoner = yes
			practical_age >= 5
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			is_murder_quest_target_of_root_trigger = no
		}

		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power >= 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT

# Prison Break - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7765
	desc = EVTDESC7765
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7765 # Tries to escape

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = craven }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7766 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7773 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7773 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7767 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7774 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7774 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7765 # Does not try to escape

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = craven }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7768 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7775 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7775 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7769 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7776 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7776 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bathtub Drowning - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7785
	desc = EVTDESC7785
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7785 # Drowns

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_strong_trigger = yes }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { is_weak_trigger = yes }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7786 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7793 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7793 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7787 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7794 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7794 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7785 # Does not drown

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_strong_trigger = yes }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { is_weak_trigger = yes }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7788 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7795 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7795 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7789 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7796 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7796 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bathtub Drowning - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7786
	desc = EVTDESC7786
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7786

		if = {
			limit = { is_alive = yes }

			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = event_target:plot_leader
			}
		}
	}
}

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {

		if = {
			limit = { is_alive = yes }

			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_unknown_drowning
				killer = event_target:plot_leader
			}
		}
	}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Boating Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7800
	desc = EVTDESC7800
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	portrait = event_target:plot_target

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}

		is_plot_active = no

		plot_target_char = {
			is_adult = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			practical_age > 5
			is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
			is_murder_quest_target_of_root_trigger = no
		}

			plotter = ROOT

		}
	}

			factor = 0.9

			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.90
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 1.5
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 1.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 1.5
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 2.0
		}

		# CK2Plus
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 3.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 4.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 6.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 8.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 10.0
		}
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.60
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying2
		}

		mult_modifier = {

			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying3

			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying5

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			plot_target_char = {
				has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network

				check_variable = {
					which = personal_spy_network
					value >= 10
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

# Boating Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7805
	desc = EVTDESC7805
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7805 # Drowns

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_strong_trigger = yes }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { is_weak_trigger = yes }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7806 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7813 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7813 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7807 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7814 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7814 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7805 # Does not drown

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_strong_trigger = yes }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { is_weak_trigger = yes }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7808 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7815 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7815 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7809 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7816 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7816 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### POISONOUS SNAKE
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisonous Snake
character_event = {
	id = 7820
	desc = EVTDESC7820
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	portrait = event_target:plot_target

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}

		is_plot_active = no

		plot_target_char = {
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			block_general_event_trigger = no
			is_murder_quest_target_of_root_trigger = no
		}

		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power >= 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.10
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.20
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.30
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.40
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.50
			}
		}

				plotter = ROOT

		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.90
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 1.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 1.5
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 2.0
		}

		# CK2Plus
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 3.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 4.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 6.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 8.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 10.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

# Poisonous Snake - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7825
	desc = EVTDESC7825
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_target_of = event_target:plot_leader


		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7825 # Drowns

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = craven }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = slothful }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7826 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7827 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7825 # Does not drown

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = craven }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = slothful }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7828 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7835 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7835 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7829 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7836 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7836 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### BALCONY PLUMMET
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Balcony Plummet
character_event = {
	id = 7840
	desc = EVTDESC7840
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	portrait = event_target:plot_target

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}

		is_plot_active = no

		plot_target_char = {
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			block_general_event_trigger = no
			is_murder_quest_target_of_root_trigger = no
		}

		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power >= 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.10
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.20
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.30
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.40
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.50
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.60
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.70
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.80
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 0.90
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.9

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power >= 1.5
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 1.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 1.5
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 2.0
		}

		# CK2Plus
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 3.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 4.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 6.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 8.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power >= 10.0
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.60
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying2
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.45
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying3
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.30
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying4
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.15
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying5
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			plot_target_char = {
				has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network

				check_variable = {
					which = personal_spy_network
					value >= 10
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			plot_target_char = {
				has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network

				check_variable = {
					which = personal_spy_network
					value >= 20
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			plot_target_char = {
				has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network

				check_variable = {
					which = personal_spy_network
					value >= 30
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			plot_target_char = {
				has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network

				check_variable = {
					which = personal_spy_network
					value >= 40
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			plot_target_char = {
				has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network

				check_variable = {
					which = personal_spy_network
					value >= 50
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = plot_leader

		plot_target_char = {
			save_event_target_as = plot_target
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7840 # The conspirators bribe the servants

		trigger = { plot_power >= 1.0 }

		any_plot_backer = {
			character_event = {
				id = 7852 # Inform
				days = 1
			}
		}

		activate_plot = yes

		event_target:plot_target = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 7845
				days = 30
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7845
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7840 # Bribe servants

		trigger = {
			plot_power < 0.5
			intrigue < 10
		}

		scaled_wealth = -1.0

		any_plot_backer = {
			character_event = {
				id = 7852 # Inform
				days = 1
			}
		}

		activate_plot = yes

		event_target:plot_target = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 7845
				days = 30
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7845
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7840 # Bribe servants

		trigger = {
			plot_power >= 0.5
			plot_power < 1.0
			intrigue < 10
		}

		scaled_wealth = -0.5

		any_plot_backer = {
			character_event = {
				id = 7852 # Inform
				days = 1
			}
		}

		activate_plot = yes

		event_target:plot_target = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 7845
				days = 30
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7845
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC7840 # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = intrigue

		trigger = {
			plot_power >= 0.5
			intrigue >= 10
		}

		any_plot_backer = {
			character_event = {
				id = 7852 # Inform
				days = 1
			}
		}

		activate_plot = yes

		event_target:plot_target = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 7845
				days = 30
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP7845
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD8150 # I cannot afford this

		trigger = {
			intrigue < 10
			plot_power < 1.0
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

# Balcony Plummet - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7845
	desc = EVTDESC7845
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7845 # Drowns

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7846 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7853 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7853 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7847 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7854 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7854 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7845 # Does not drown

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7848 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7855 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7855 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7849 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7856 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7856 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### HUNTING ACCIDENT - CHILDREN ONLY
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Hunting Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7860
	desc = EVTDESC7860
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	portrait = event_target:plot_target

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}

					is_adult = no
					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}

				plot_target_char = {
					check_variable = {
						which = personal_spy_network
						value >= 40
					}

					has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network
					is_adult = no
					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.1

			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}

				plot_target_char = {
					check_variable = {
						which = personal_spy_network
						value >= 50
					}

					has_character_flag = has_personal_spy_network
					is_adult = no
					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = plot_backer

		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}

				is_plot_active = no
				plot_power >= 0.5

				plot_target_char = {
					is_adult = no
					practical_age >= 5
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = no
				}

				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV
						power >= 0.025
					}
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = plot_leader

			plot_target_char = {
				save_event_target_as = plot_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7860 # The conspirators bribe servants

		trigger = {
			event_target:plot_leader = {
				plot_power >= 1.0
			}
		}

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			show_scope_change = no

			activate_plot = yes

			character_event = {
				id = 7870
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8160
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8151 # Ask the Plotter for funds

		trigger = {
			intrigue < 10

			event_target:plot_leader = {
				plot_power < 1.0
			}
		}

		event_target:plot_leader = {
			show_scope_change = no

			activate_plot = yes

			character_event = {
				id = 7862
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8152
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7860 # Bribe servants

				plot_power < 1.0
			}
		}

# Hunting Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7865
	desc = EVTDESC7865
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7865 # Drowns

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = gregarious }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7866 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7873 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7873 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7867 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7874 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7874 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7865 # Does not drown

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = gregarious }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7868 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7875 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7875 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7869 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7876 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7876 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
