# Disguised Highwaymen - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7885
	desc = EVTDESC7885
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7885 # Drowns

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7886 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7893 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7893 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7887 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7894 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7894 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7885 # Does not drown

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7888 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7895 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7895 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7889 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7896 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7896 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Disguised Highwaymen - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7886
	desc = EVTDESC7886
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7886

		if = {
			limit = { is_alive = yes }

			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = event_target:plot_leader
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = {

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Carriage Accident
character_event = {

# Carriage Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7905
	desc = EVTDESC7905
	picture = GFX_evt_carriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7905 # Drowns

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7906 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7913 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7913 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7907 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7914 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7914 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7905 # Does not drown

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = paranoid }
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = diligent }
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = trusting }
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random > 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7908 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7915 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7915 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7909 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7916 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7916 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 7952
	desc = EVTDESC8152

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = EVTOPTA8152

			value = 1.0
		}

		event_target:plot_backer = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 7953
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8153
			}
		}
	}

		name = EVTOPTB8152
		event_target:plot_backer = {
			show_scope_change = no

# Decadent Debauchery - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7955
	desc = EVTDESC7955
	picture = GFX_evt_jugglers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			is_plot_active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7955 # Dies

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = slothful
						trait = proud
					}
				}
				random < 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = hedonist
						trait = gluttonous
					}
				}
				random < 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = drunkard
						trait = lustful
					}
				}
				random < 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random < 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7956 # Dies, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7963 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7963 days = 1 } }
				}

				75 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7957 # Dies, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7964 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7964 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB7955 # Does not die

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = slothful
						trait = proud
					}
				}
				random >= 33
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = hedonist
						trait = gluttonous
					}
				}
				random >= 50
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = drunkard
						trait = lustful
					}
				}
				random >= 90
			}
			trigger_else = {
				random >= 75
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7958 # Lives, murderer discovered
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7965 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7965 days = 1 } }
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 7959 # Lives, murderer unknown
						days = 1
					}

					# Notify
					event_target:plot_leader = { character_event = { id = 7966 days = 1 } }
					event_target:plot_backer = { character_event = { id = 7966 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - antiking
letter_event = {
	id = 8200
	desc = EVTDESC8200

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_antiking }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes

			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_antiking

				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000

		hidden_effect = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					vassal_of = ROOT

					NOR = {
						in_faction = faction_antiking
						character = ROOT
					}
				}

				character_event = { id = 8202 }
			}

			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8203 }
				diplomatic_immunity = no

				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_antiking

					letter_event = { id = 8201 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			religion_authority = {
				name = deposed_antipope
				years = 50
			}

			faction_antiking = { # The target (title) of the faction
				set_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss

				if = {
					limit = { has_law = investiture_law_1 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = investiture_law_0
				}

				clr_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				religion_head = {
					opinion = {
						name = opinion_deposed_antipope
						who = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			rightful_religious_head_scope = {
				remove_claim = k_papacy
				remove_claim = d_fraticelli
			}
		}

		primary_title = {
			show_scope_change = no

			usurp_title = FROM
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5

			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_antiking
						power >= 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8000

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_antiking
							power >= 1.0
						}
					}
				}

				random = {
					chance = 25

					character_event = {
						id = 45002 # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
						months = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = {
				id = 8204
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8100
			}

			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_antiking
					count = 10
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_antiking
							power < 0.75
						}
					}

					random_list = {
						50 = { }

						30 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45000 # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}

						20 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45004 # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_antiking
							power < 1.5
						}
					}

					random_list = {
						75 = { }

						5 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45000 # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}

						20 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45004 # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.75

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_antiking
						power >= 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {

# Ultimatum - increase council power
letter_event = {
	id = 8215
	desc = EVTDESC8215

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_increase_council_power }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes

			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_increase_council_power

				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000

		hidden_effect = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					vassal_of = ROOT

					NOR = {
						in_faction = faction_increase_council_power
						character = ROOT
					}
				}

				character_event = { id = 8217 }
			}

			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8218 }
				diplomatic_immunity = no

				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_increase_council_power

					letter_event = { id = 8216 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_increased_council_power
				who = ROOT
				months = 12
			}

			faction_increase_council_power = { # The target (title) of the faction
				increase_council_power_effect = yes
				increase_vassal_freedom_effect = yes
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_increase_council_power
						power < 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8000

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_increase_council_power
							power >= 1.0
						}
					}
				}

				random = {
					chance = 25

					character_event = {
						id = 45002 # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
						months = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = {
				id = 8219
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8100
			}

			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_increase_council_power
					count = 10
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_increase_council_power
							power < 0.75
						}
					}

					random_list = {
						50 = { }

						30 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45000 # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}

						20 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45004 # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_increase_council_power
							power < 1.5
						}
					}

					random_list = {
						75 = { }

						5 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45000 # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}

						20 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45004 # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 8

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				war = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_increase_council_power
						power >= 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_increase_council_power
						power >= 1.5
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.35

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_increase_council_power
						power >= 2.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.2

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_increase_council_power
						power >= 3.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.2

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_increase_council_power
						power >= 4.0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
 }

# Inform faction backer - increase council power
letter_event = {
	id = 8216
	desc = EVTDESC8216

	show_from_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = GOOD

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_grateful
			who = FROMFROM
			years = 5
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = faction_council_power_ultimatum_timer
			years = 10
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

# Inform other vassals - increase council power
character_event = {
	id = 8217
	desc = EVTDESC8217
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	show_from_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	notification = yes

	ai = no

	option = {
		name = I_SEE
	}
}

# Demand accepted - increase council power
letter_event = {
	id = 8218
	desc = EVTDESC8218

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT

		clr_character_flag = faction_council_power_ultimatum_taken

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = faction_council_power_ultimatum_timer
			years = 10
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

# Demand rejected - increase council power
letter_event = {
	id = 8219
	desc = EVTDESC8100

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8100

		clr_character_flag = faction_council_power_ultimatum_taken

		faction_increase_council_power = { # The target (title) of the faction
			show_scope_change = no

			reverse_war = {
				target = ROOT
				casus_belli = increase_council_power_war
				faction = faction_increase_council_power
			}
		}
	}
 }

# Ultimatum - powerful vassal takeover
letter_event = {
	id = 8220
	desc = EVTDESC8220

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes

			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover

				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}

		most_popular_vassal = {
			limit = {
				higher_real_tier_than = BARON
				is_feudal = yes
				is_adult = yes

				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_female = yes }

					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_law = true_cognatic_succession
							has_law = enatic_cognatic_succession
							has_law = enatic_succession
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_law = true_cognatic_succession
							has_law = cognatic_succession
							has_law = agnatic_succession
						}
					}
				}

				prisoner = no
				is_incapable = no
				NOT = { trait = eunuch }
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = new_title_holder
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000

		hidden_effect = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					vassal_of = ROOT

					NOR = {
						in_faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
						character = ROOT
					}
				}

				character_event = { id = 8222 }
			}

			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8223 }
				diplomatic_immunity = no

				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover

					letter_event = { id = 8221 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_abdicated
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			faction_powerful_vassal_takeover = { # The target (title) of the faction
				event_target:new_title_holder = {
					show_scope_change = no

					usurp_title = {
						target = PREV
						type = faction_demand
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						job_chancellor = { remove_title = job_chancellor }
						job_marshal = { remove_title = job_marshal }
						job_treasurer = { remove_title = job_treasurer }
						job_spymaster = { remove_title = job_spymaster }
						job_spiritual = { remove_title = job_spiritual }
					}
				}

				increase_council_power_effect = yes
				increase_vassal_freedom_effect = yes
				increase_vassal_freedom_effect = yes

				set_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss

				if = {
					limit = { has_law = succession_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = succession_voting_power_1
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						trigger_if = {
							limit = {
								has_law = law_voting_power_1
								has_law = war_voting_power_1
								has_law = grant_title_voting_power_1
								has_law = revoke_title_voting_power_1
								has_law = imprison_voting_power_1
								has_law = banish_voting_power_1
								has_law = execution_voting_power_1
							}

							NOR = {
								has_law = succ_feudal_elective
								has_law = succ_byzantine_elective
								has_law = succ_hre_elective
							}
						}
						trigger_else = {
							NOT = { has_law = succ_gavelkind }
						}
					}

					custom_tooltip = {
						text = overthrow_text

						# Change to elective if possible, gavelkind otherwise
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_law = law_voting_power_1
								has_law = war_voting_power_1
								has_law = grant_title_voting_power_1
								has_law = revoke_title_voting_power_1
								has_law = imprison_voting_power_1
								has_law = banish_voting_power_1
								has_law = execution_voting_power_1
							}

							if = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										title = e_byzantium
										title = e_roman_empire
										has_title_flag = alternate_byz
									}
								}

								add_law_w_cooldown = succ_byzantine_elective
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										title = e_hre
										has_title_flag = alternate_hre
									}
								}

								add_law_w_cooldown = succ_hre_elective
							}
							else = {
								add_law_w_cooldown = succ_feudal_elective
							}
						}
						else = {
							add_law_w_cooldown = succ_gavelkind
						}
					}
				}

				clr_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
						power >= 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB8000

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
							power >= 1.0
						}
					}
				}

				random = {
					chance = 25

					character_event = {
						id = 45002 # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
						months = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			letter_event = {
				id = 8224
				days = 3
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP8100
			}

			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
					count = 10
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
							power < 0.75
						}
					}

					random_list = {
						50 = { }

						30 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45000 # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}

						20 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45004 # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
							power < 1.5
						}
					}

					random_list = {
						75 = { }

						5 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45000 # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}

						20 = {
							character_event = {
								id = 45004 # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
								days = 17
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.75

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
						power >= 1.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
						power >= 1.5
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
						power >= 2.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
						power >= 3.0
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover
						power >= 4.0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform faction backer - Powerful Vassal Takeover
letter_event = {
	id = 8221
	desc = evt_CK2_8221_desc_a

	show_from_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = GOOD

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_grateful
			who = FROMFROM
			years = 5
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { character = event_target:new_title_holder }
			}

			add_favor = event_target:new_title_holder

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_favorite
				who = event_target:new_title_holder
				years = 5
			}
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover_ultimatum_timer
			years = 10
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
 }

# Inform other vassals - Powerful Vassal Takeover

	notification = yes
	show_from_from = yes

		name = I_SEE
	}
 }

letter_event = {
	id = 8223
	desc = EVTDESC8223

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT

		clr_character_flag = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover_ultimatum_taken

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { character = event_target:new_title_holder }
			}

			add_favor = event_target:new_title_holder

			opinion = {
				who = event_target:new_title_holder
				name = opinion_favorite
				years = 5
			}
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover_ultimatum_timer
			years = 10
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
 }

# Winning war notification - Powerful Vassal Takeover
letter_event = {
	id = 8225
	desc = EVTDESC8225

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = helped_win_war
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8225

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_favorite
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}

		add_favor = FROM
	}
}

# Winning war notification - New title holder
character_event = {
	id = 8226
	desc = EVTDESC8226
	picture = GFX_evt_coronation
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		primary_title = {
			set_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss

			if = {
				limit = { has_law = succession_voting_power_0 }
				add_law_w_cooldown = succession_voting_power_1
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR =  {
						has_law = succ_feudal_elective
						has_law = succ_byzantine_elective
						has_law = succ_hre_elective
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							title = e_byzantium
							title = e_roman_empire
							has_title_flag = alternate_byz
						}
					}

					add_law_w_cooldown = succ_byzantine_elective
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							title = e_hre
							has_title_flag = alternate_hre
						}
					}

					add_law_w_cooldown = succ_hre_elective
				}
				else = {
					add_law_w_cooldown = succ_feudal_elective
				}
			}

			clr_title_flag = non_manual_law_change # No prestige loss
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8226

		job_chancellor = {
			show_scope_change = no
			remove_title = job_chancellor
		}

		job_marshal = {
			show_scope_change = no
			remove_title = job_marshal
		}

		job_treasurer = {
			show_scope_change = no
			remove_title = job_treasurer
		}

		job_spymaster = {
			show_scope_change = no
			remove_title = job_spymaster
		}

		job_spiritual = {
			show_scope_change = no
			remove_title = job_spiritual
		}

		any_vassal = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = helped_win_war }

			letter_event = { id = 8225 days = 1 }

			tooltip = {
				opinion = {
					name = opinion_favorite
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}

				reverse_add_favor = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}
